I kind of loved this place. Tiny unassuming shack by the side of the road with a limited no-nonsense menu, outdoor seating, no alcohol permitted. We saw a bunch of locals come and go with their favorite orders - people order, eat, and leave. He said they could do it but some of it is based off credit, so we had him run his credit and Victor said my business partner score was too low and what they would like to do is, set us up on a short term loan with a high pay back based off of our deposits. I told him there "no reason" for us todo that cause we didn't need a small loan but need a larger loan to buy me out and expand (around 100k) and if we can't do that, don't worry about it. Victor tells us we can't get that one at the time but what we can do is, get a smaller one (15k) with a payback of 3 months and it's just to establish a relationship with the bank and once they see good payment history, they will lend us the larger amount. And he goes on to say, we don't even have to wait the full 3 months, if the history is good after two months we can just get it refinanced at that point. I told him I would get back with him n a few days after we did our due diligence. We did-looked up the company, looked at reviews, looked on bbb and nothing came back/alarmed us, so we went with it.

<user_name>Michael Cook< /user_name><userid>116261873171225440105</userid>< gmap_id>

<Response>None</Response>< Text>
I am a student at Fresno State and am originally from Texas. I love Fr. David and Deacon John. The church itself, although not my favorite style architecturally speaking, is beautiful although I wish the tabernacle was in more plain view. I enjoy when the organ is utilized in the liturgy. I wish that the center would be a little more active in campus life but realize that it can be very difficult. The primary reason as to why I regularly attend St. Anthony's over this center is the fact that first, the faithful seem to be disengaged during the Mass and you can frequently hear people having conversations with each other before, during, and after Mass. Second, there are no kneelers and it seems that Deacon John has no interest in installing them. Although this may sound trivial, the consecration of the Holy Eucharist demands the most reverent of stances from the faithful and standing up, as if we were in line for ice cream, does not seem very reverent to me. Other than that I am thankful for this center and am thankful for what this Church offers to the campus and community.</Text>

I also started getting my eyebrows done here a few years ago and for $7 I get more compliments on them than the $50+ job I used to get at Anastasia in Beverly Hills< /Text>

<Response>None<//Response><UserId.>101310301169682792401</UserId.>< review>
My first time going to B&J nails was a great experience! I decided to try it for a mani/pedi because it's close to my house so an easy walk and had good reviews and prices online.
I called around 10 to make sure they were open because sometimes this isn't the case around here (listed hours online not matching actual hours of operation) and they answered pretty fast to let me know they were open and taking walkins and gave me the prices. I walked in  around 10:15 and they were able to help me right away. The woman who did my toes was a total pro and cut trimmed and buffed my feet and nails without any pain and got rid of a LOT (I'm ashamed to say) gunk! Another woman came to do my fingernails after my pedi was over and she was quick and thorough! I was finished with both mani/pedi and drying by 5 to 11 so I wasn't even there for an hour! Everyone there seems to be experts not only at nails but in customer service!
The only bad review I'd have is of a couple of customers there while I was that were constantly complaining. I don't care to go too deeply into it but both customers were over the top rude and were still treated with respect and patience.
I will definitely be returning here and see if the experience is always so stellar<//review>

<Time>1452566134303<//Time><rating>4<//rating>< Review>
I really wanted to go to Joe's because of its quirky exterior and the commercials made it seem like the food/servings were fresh and abundant as well as a great value - sucker!  To start, I had the steamed shrimp appetizer for around $10.  I expected tiger size shrimp but instead they were the small cocktail size shrimp (10), so it was like $1 a shrimp.  For the entree we got 2 buckets of crab, having ordered one at first, we knew it would not be enough for two, we ordered another.

The seasoning is good, but the price is not right.  For the above and a pitcher of beer I ended up paying nearly $100.< /Review>

NOOOOTTTTT!!!!!! it took a few mins to get seated which seemed odd since the place was practically deserted which should've raised RED FLAGS! The service was horrible from our server! we had asked for numerous items and which none were brought to us by our server. We had to ask the other servers for items like dip for three of our children which took ten min to obtain ranch dressing. Also i had asked for crab crackers and they said that they didnt have any available. WTF???? no crab crackers at JOE'S CRAB SHACK??? Then i asked another server and they said they will get us a pair they were washing them. 15 min later we received the cracker. By the time we were ready to eat our food (us the parents) our 4 children had devoured their food and were on the play ground or what i like to call "a parents nightmare" almost all the playground equipment was made out of metal/steel and the ground was covered with pebbles. If you are wanting to enjoy a meal do not go outside with your kids to the playground. Kids were throwing pebbles and i ask our children to come back to the table since the only supervision is you.

And did i mention it was our 6yr old sons birthday?? I had told the server when we were being seated that it was his birthday. She asked which one and i pointed him out. ( we chose to sit outdoors in front of the playground, so the kids walked straight to the play equipment ) My husband mentioned it to the server and the neighboring server that was helping us, that it is our little guys big day. The kids and i were in the restroom getting the dust washed off from the playground and i was hoping they would sing "Happy Birthday" to our son  just like they did to  a neighboring party. Nope we just sat there waiting now for the check. By this time i am Pissed! We have been ignored and we had spent over two hrs there! We did not enjoy our meal since they we not prepared for customers needs. I asked for the check and let them know how disappointed i was in their service and that we will not be returning in the future. The manager came to our table ten min after i gave a server our payment. He said what can i do to make things right? I said what can you do? We just want to leave. He tried to give us a gift card but i did not take it. I told him why would we want to come back?

We actually had plans afterwards to go have cake with Grandparents and cousins but because the service was so slow we were going to be really late. So we just told them we will do it tomorrow. The birthday boy will have a treat and will be sung happy birthday to at Joe's i told them. What a joke! we ended up going to Yogurtland on the way home. < Name>
Donnah Smith</Name>
< Text>
Very tasty; not too salty. I had the fish sandwich (grilled white fish). The dill tartar sauce is light and the perfect accompaniment, as is the buttered bun. The other item order was the grilled fish burrito. My partner really enjoyed the flavor. Again not too salty. Maybe a little dry for me. Good price point for the quality and the atmosphere on the patio. Feels like a little tropical patio. I added the side + drink for $3.95 more. Got the grilled zucchini. 4 thick slices with a nice char. I wouldn't have mind a little additional salt here, but again very fresh and light tasting. The burrito was huge. Everything was filling. This is a walk-up and order spot that delivers your food to your table. They did a good job of checking up on us without being overbearing. The patio tables were a little close to truly be six feet apart in my opinion, but it wasn't crowded, so we were able to distance ourselves from others a little bit. I would def return if I'm in the area craving a light, quick seafood meal.</Text>

<Gmap_id>0x80dd313c5c39586f:0x43eca0c0d599585a< /Gmap_id>< Text>
Finally made it inside to try the food, and it was a pleasant surprise! The food is so so good!

I had the Salmon with sweet potato fries. These guys really know how to use a grill! The vibe is really great too. Vintage long Beach photos, nautical theme objects litter the walls. The chairs and table are also very unique and interesting.

The outdoor seating area is spacial and had nice views of Downtown Long Beach even overlooking the Convention center and further away Rainbow Harbor.

The restrooms here are super nice. The staff are friendly and helpful.

I walked here so I don't know how the parking is. I can only imagine paid with possible validation. Park somewhere else and walk, it's worth it and it's also a nice walk.<//Text>

<UserId.>108743264813652782343< /UserId.>< time>
1445289584438</time>
< review>
Decided to head to downtown Long Beach and had a craving for fish and chips. Couldn't find a fried fish place to my liking but Pier76 had a great sounding menu of grilled fish and the like. It was a hit! It's a casual dining place but with a more contemporary class than your standard fish shack. It reminded me a lot of California Fish Grill. Perfectly grilled fish with an array of delicious creams and sauces to accent each fish. Good serving size and comes with buttery rice and choice of one side. Their fountain drinks have a selection of quality soda by Stubborn specialty soda company and two Izze flavors. I stay away from standard high fructose syrup sodas so it was a nice treat to have this selection. Prices are also reasonable for what tastes like good quality fish!<//review>

5</rate>
< Review>
Came here for an early family lunch after a harbor cruise and were delighted with the find.

1) Free 2 hours parking validated by the restaurant at the lot that's about a 5ft walk away.

2) I was worried that it might be difficult to get a table for 10 but the staff had pulled tables together and placed reserved signs on them for our group.

3) Ordering food was quick and easy, despite the size of our group. You order up at the counter and they have a nice vintage chic sea type seating area. Very cozy and aesthetically pleasing, like SF restaurants.

4) Free regular lemonade if you check in on Yelp! It was really tasty. Or you can choose from draft beers or Craft Soda from the fountain.

5) Food came out pretty fast. (I wish they would've given cutlery to everyone though.) All the dishes were large serving sizes so we ended up sharing quite a bit. Everything I ate was delicious! The clam chowder, calamari in a sweet tangy sauce with a carrot type coleslaw. The lobster roll was the only entree that came with a free drink. The beer battered fish and chips was awesome, and the fish didn't taste too heavy despite being fried. The grilled fish entrees with rice and sides were very tasty and good healthy options. No one ordered the Maine lobster at our table, but other patrons did and it looked awesome. We were all very pleased with the food.

6) Service was great. Nice, clean place. Not too loud and good central location. Nice patio seating to be used in warmer weather.

7) Overall, fabulous experience.</Review>

My friends and I had the lobster roll, mac and cheese, oysters, and the broccoli and brussels sprouts.
I am not sure why the lobster rolls were so highly beloved. for me, it was just okay. I felt like it did not come all together for me. Oysters of course were good and big as well. The mac and cheese was super disappointing. I felt that it was dry, congealed looking and tasted like it lacked true flavor. I actually really enjoyed the broccoli and brussels sprouts. I thought it was well cooked and well flavored. If i were ever to come back, it would be for that. I also had the cucumber mint lemonade which i felt had great flavor, was refreshing and great combination of sweet and sour.

The best part about this place is the alcohol, the drinks, atmosphere inside and out and the broccoli and brussels sprouts.< /review>

<review>Soo so good. It's rare to find a fast casual place with lots of seafood choices. I find most sit-down seafood restaurants intimidating because I don't know much about seafood.

I had grilled tilapia with grilled zucchini as my side. I paid extra for brown rice and even that tasted extra good - I think they cook it in something savory. The tilapia came with an aioli that presented me with a dilemma: eat the deliciously grilled tilapia without the yummy decadent aioli or eat the aioli with the tilapia and miss the perfect solo flavor of the fish. I might have had some aioli-covered fork as a third choice.

I added a side of the kale tomato salad. Heads up: when ordered a la carte, the side is huge. Almost entree size. Also delicious.

Can't wait to try more things!< /review><pictures>None</pictures><Response>None<//Response>< gmap_id>
